# Weapons (All)

This page exists for easy comparison of the basic attributes of [base](Skyrim_Weapons.md), [specialty](Skyrim_Specialty_Gear.md), [artifact](Skyrim_Artifacts.md), [unique](Skyrim_Unique_Weapons.md), [quest](Skyrim_Quest_Items.md), [Ancient Nord](Skyrim_Ancient_Nord.md), [Forsworn](Skyrim_Forsworn_Equipment.md), [Falmer](Skyrim_Falmer_Equipment.md), and [Creation Club](Skyrim_Creation_Club.md) weapons the player can normally use. For additional general weapon information, see the [base weapons page](Skyrim_Weapons.md). To compare arrows and bolts, see [Ammunition](Skyrim_Ammunition.md). For information regarding enchantments, tempering, and leveled versions, click a weapon name to view the corresponding page.

### Warhammers
- **Reach**: 1.3
- **Speed**: 0.6 (0.8 for [The Longhammer](Skyrim_The_Longhammer.md))
- **Stagger**: 1.25 (1.35 for [Stalhrim Warhammer](Skyrim_Stalhrim_Warhammer.md))
